[30;1m72 | [0m[35m``SChunk`` is a simple data container that handles setting, expanding and[0m
[30;1m73 | [0m[35mgetting data and metadata.  In contrast to chunks, a super-chunk can update[0m
[30;1m74 | [0m[35mand resize the data that it contains, supports user metadata, and has virtually[0m
[30;1m75 | [0m[35munlimited storage capacity (chunks, on the other hand, cannot store more than 2 GB).[0m
[30;1m76 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m77 | [0m[35mAdditionally, you can convert a SChunk into a contiguous, serialized buffer[0m
